  27 
  28 ------tab.pl
  29 
  30     $n=0;
  31 
  32    while (<>) {
  33      local($uhc, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
  34      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
  35      local($k)=hex($uhc);
  36      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 8 eq 0);
  37      ++$n;
  38      printf (" 0x%04x,", $u);
  39    }
  40    printf ("\n");

3037 /* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function.  */
3038 #define CHARSET_NAME        "UHC//"
3039 #define FROM_LOOP       from_uhc
3040 #define TO_LOOP         to_uhc
3041 #define DEFINE_INIT     1
3042 #define DEFINE_FINI     1
3043 #define MIN_NEEDED_FROM     1
3044 #define MAX_NEEDED_FROM     2
3045 #define MIN_NEEDED_TO       4
3046 #define ONE_DIRECTION       0
3047 
3048 /* First define the conversion function from UHC to UCS4.  */
3049 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_FROM
3050 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_FROM
3051 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_TO
3052 #define LOOPFCT         FROM_LOOP
3053 #define BODY \
3054   {                                       \
3055     uint32_t ch = (uint32_t) *inptr;                          \
3056                                           \
3057 /* half-width Korean Currency WON sign                        \
3058                                           \
3059     if (ch == 0x5c)                               \
3060       ch =  0x20a9;                               \
3061     else if (ch <= 0x7f)                              \
3062       ch = (uint32_t) ch;                             \
3063 */                                        \
3064     if (ch <= 0x7f)                               \
3065       ++inptr;                                    \
3066     else if (__builtin_expect (ch <= 0x80, 0)                     \
3067          || __builtin_expect (ch >= 0xfe, 0)                  \
3068          || __builtin_expect (ch == 0xc9, 0))                 \
3069       {                                       \
3070     /* This is illegal.  */                           \
3071     STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
3072       }                                       \
3073     else                                      \
3074       {                                       \
3075     /* Two-byte character.  First test whether the next byte          \
3076        is also available.  */                         \
3077     uint32_t ch2;                                 \
3078                                           \
3079     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
3080       {                                   \
3081         /* The second character is not available.  Store              \
3082            the intermediate result.  */                   \
3083         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
3084         break;                                \
3085       }                                   \
3086                                           \
3087     ch2 = inptr[1];                               \
3088                                           \
3089 /*                                        \
3090   Additional code points not present in EUC-KR                    \
3091                                           \
3092          1st byte             2nd byte                        \
3093      0x81-0xa0            0x41-0x5a, 0x61-0x7a, 0x81-0xfe         total       \
3094       (32)                 (26)   +    (26)   +    (126) = 178     5696       \
3095                                           \
3096      0xa1-0xc5            0x41-0x5a  0x61-0x7a  0x81-0xa0             \
3097       (37)                  (26)  +   (26)    +    (32) =  84      3108       \
3098                                           \
3099      0xc6                 0x41-0x52                       \
3100       (1)                    (18)                                   18        \
3101                                           \
3102                                                                     8822      \
3103                                           \
3104   8822(only in UHC) + 2350(both in EUC-KR and UHC) =  11,172              \
3105 */                                        \
3106                                           \
3107     if (ch < 0xa1 || ch2 < 0xa1)                          \
3108       {                                   \
3109         if (__builtin_expect (ch > 0xc6, 0)                   \
3110         || __builtin_expect (ch2 < 0x41, 0)               \
3111         || __builtin_expect (ch2 > 0xfe, 0)               \
3112         || (__builtin_expect (ch2 > 0x5a, 0) && ch2 < 0x61)       \
3113         || (__builtin_expect (ch2 > 0x7a, 0) && ch2 < 0x81)       \
3114         || (__builtin_expect (ch == 0xc6, 0) && ch2 > 0x52))          \
3115           {                                   \
3116         /* This is not legal.  */                     \
3117         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);               \
3118           }                                   \
3119                                           \
3120         ch = uhc_extra_to_ucs[ch2 - 0x41                      \
3121                  - (ch2 > 0x80 ? 12 : (ch2 > 0x60 ? 6 : 0))   \
3122                  +  (ch < 0xa1                    \
3123                      ? (ch - 0x81) * 178              \
3124                      : 5696 + (ch - 0xa1) * 84)];         \
3125                                           \
3126         if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == 0))                   \
3127           {                                   \
3128         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
3129         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2);               \
3130           }                                   \
3131                                           \
3132         inptr += 2;                               \
3133       }                                   \
3134     else                                      \
3135       {                                   \
3136         ch = ksc5601_to_ucs4 (&inptr, 2, 0x80);               \
3137         if (__builtin_expect (ch == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR, 0)          \
3138         || __builtin_expect (ch == 0x327e, 0))                \
3139           {                                   \
3140         /* Illegal.  */                           \
3141         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2);               \
3142           }                                   \
3143       }                                   \
3144       }                                       \
3145                                           \
3146     put32 (outptr, ch);                               \
3147     outptr += 4;                                  \
3148   }
3149 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
3150 #define ONEBYTE_BODY \
3151   {                                       \
3152     if (c < 0x80)                                 \
3153       return c;                                   \
3154     else                                      \
3155       return WEOF;                                \
3156   }
3157 #include <iconv/loop.c>
3158 
3159 
3160 /* Next, define the other direction.  */
3161 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_TO
3162 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_FROM
3163 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_FROM
3164 #define LOOPFCT         TO_LOOP
3165 #define BODY \
3166   {                                       \
3167     uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr);                          \
3168                                           \
3169     if (ch <= 0x7f)                               \
3170       /* XXX Think about 0x5c ; '\'.  */                      \
3171       *outptr++ = ch;                                 \
3172     else if (ch >= 0xac00 && ch <= 0xd7a3)                    \
3173       {                                       \
3174     const char *s = uhc_hangul_from_ucs[ch - 0xac00];             \
3175                                           \
3176     if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 2 > outend))               \
3177       {                                   \
3178         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
3179         break;                                \
3180       }                                   \
3181                                           \
3182     *outptr++ = s[0];                             \
3183     *outptr++ = s[1];                             \
3184       }                                       \
3185     else if ((ch >= 0x4e00 && ch <= 0x9fa5) || (ch >= 0xf900 && ch <= 0xfa0b))\
3186       {                                       \
3187     size_t written = ucs4_to_ksc5601_hanja (ch, outptr, outend - outptr); \
3188                                           \
3189     if (__glibc_unlikely (written == 0))                      \
3190       {                                   \
3191         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
3192         break;                                \
3193       }                                   \
3194     if (__glibc_unlikely (written == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR))           \
3195       {                                   \
3196         STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4);                     \
3197       }                                   \
3198                                           \
3199     *outptr++ |= 0x80;                            \
3200     *outptr++ |= 0x80;                            \
3201       }                                       \
3202 /* Half-width Korean Currency Won Sign                        \
3203       else if (ch == 0x20a9)                              \
3204         idx = 0x5c00;                                 \
3205 */                                        \
3206     else                                      \
3207       {                                       \
3208     size_t written = ucs4_to_ksc5601_sym (ch, outptr, outend - outptr);   \
3209                                           \
3210     if (__builtin_expect (ch == 0x327e, 0)                    \
3211         || __builtin_expect (written == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR, 0))         \
3212       {                                   \
3213         UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4);                      \
3214         STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4);                     \
3215       }                                   \
3216     if (__glibc_unlikely (written == 0))                      \
3217       {                                   \
3218         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
3219         break;                                \
3220       }                                   \
3221                                           \
3222     *outptr++ |= 0x80;                            \
3223     *outptr++ |= 0x80;                            \
3224       }                                       \
3225                                           \
3226     inptr += 4;                                   \
3227   }
3228 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
3229 #include <iconv/loop.c>

3233 #include <iconv/skeleton.c>
